## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes Storage Subsystem CSI Driver Integration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the CSI driver integration: the CSI node plugin client, the CSI volume attach/detach controller, the CSI volume provisioner, and the PersistentVolume controller that bridges CSI operations to the core storage API.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

   - `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go` - handles provisioning/binding/recycling
   - `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller_base.go` - base framework

4. **PersistentVolume controller that bridges CSI operations to the core storage API** -

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## CSI Driver Integration Files in Kubernetes v1.32.0

### 1. CSI Node Plugin Client
- **`pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go`** — Defines the `csiClient` interface and `csiDriverClient` implementation. This is the gRPC client that communicates with CSI drivers via Unix domain sockets, wrapping all Node Service RPCs (NodeGetInfo, NodePublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, etc.).

### 2. CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller
- **`pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go`** — The `attachDetachController` watches pods/nodes and triggers attach/detach operations, with CSI migration support.
- **`pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go`** — `csiAttacher` implements `volume.Attacher`/`volume.Detacher`, creating VolumeAttachment objects and calling NodeStageVolume/NodeUnstageVolume.

### 3. CSI Volume Provisioner (PV Controller)
- **`pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go`** — Core PV controller with `CSINameTranslator` and `CSIMigratedPluginManager` interfaces for CSI migration.
